# ORION \u2014 COMPLETE LOREBASE
**The Chronicles of the Shattered Worlds**

---

## PREFACE: A RECORD IN FRAGMENTS

This chronicle compiles what is known about the worlds, the waygates, the catastrophe, and the current state of reality.

Much of what follows is **assumption built atop limited evidence**. Scholars disagree. Factions advance competing theories. New discoveries continue to undermine old conclusions.

> The truth is not lost.  
> It is unfolding.

---

# PART I: THE WORLD

## THE ANCIENT WORLD

### I. The Waygates

At the heart of every known world stands a waygate.

#### What They Are

Waygates are colossal archways formed of stone, root, and mineral, often overtaken by natural growth. At a distance, they resemble geological features shaped by erosion or time\u2014ancient cliffs worn smooth, or canyon mouths carved by forgotten rivers.

Only when approached do they reveal intentional structure, as though the land itself briefly remembered how to build.

#### How They Function

**No Interface Exists:**
- No inscriptions have ever been identified on any waygate
- No controls, levers, or mechanisms
- No interfaces or activation sequences
- All known waygates function identically

**Operation:**
- They require no activation
- They require no fuel
- They require no conscious operation
- Travelers pass through them as they would pass beneath an arch or through a canyon

**The Gate's Response:**
The gate responds automatically, reading the traveler's \u00e6theric signature and conveying them onward.

**Unknown Parameters:**
- How the destination is selected remains unknown
- The number of worlds connected by the waygate network has never been determined
- Many worlds are known; many more are suspected
- No comprehensive map exists

**Reliability:**
No recorded instance exists of a waygate malfunctioning.

#### Who Built Them

**The Builder Question:**

No verified record identifies the builders of the waygates. No ruins, tools, or cultural remnants have been conclusively linked to their construction.

It is commonly assumed that the builders are extinct, though no evidence confirms this.

**Scholarly Consensus:**

Scholars widely believe the waygates were not designed as portals in the conventional sense, but as **stabilizing anchors**\u2014structures that regulated adjacency, distance, and orientation between worlds already capable of interacting.

> **Note:** This belief is not proven, but it is consistent with post-catastrophe observations.

---

### II. The \u00c6ther

Between the worlds lies the \u00e6ther.

#### What It Is

The \u00e6ther is not empty space.

It is an active, hostile medium saturated with energies incompatible with unprotected living matter.

**Primary Property:**
Direct exposure of organic tissue to the \u00e6ther results in **total molecular disintegration**. This effect is immediate and irreversible.

#### The Elven Bride Incident

This property was confirmed beyond theoretical dispute following a historic incident that would reshape interworld politics for generations.

**The Event:**

An interworld vessel experienced a minor breach in its flux field during transit. A single strand of an elven bride's hair crossed the boundary into the \u00e6ther.

The bride died instantly.

**The Consequences:**

1. The death was initially believed to be an assassination
2. An eight-year war erupted between two elven clans
3. The true cause\u2014\u00e6theric exposure\u2014was discovered only later, during an unrelated military disaster
4. Though the war ended soon after the discovery, relations between the involved cultures never fully recovered

**What It Revealed:**

The incident proved definitively that the \u00e6ther does not merely harm. It annihilates. One strand of hair. One moment of exposure. Total death.

#### Fundamental Nature

The \u00e6ther appears indifferent rather than malicious.

It does not seek to destroy life. Rather, life appears fundamentally incompatible with it.

Whether this incompatibility is accidental or intentional remains unknown.

---

### III. Interworld Travel Beyond the Waygates

Waygates are not the only means of traveling between worlds.

#### The Interworld Vessels

Certain civilizations developed interworld vessels capable of traversing the \u00e6ther directly. These vessels vary widely in size and construction, but all rely on the same principle: **the generation of a sustained flux field**.

**The Magic Reactor:**

At the core of each vessel is a magic reactor. When activated, it projects a protective envelope around the hull, isolating everything inside from the \u00e6ther's destructive effects.

The field must be continuously maintained by trained magic users for the duration of the journey.

**The Risk:**

Failure to sustain the field results in immediate loss of all organic matter aboard.

**The Reality:**

Because of this danger, such travel is rare, resource-intensive, and politically sensitive. Only the most advanced civilizations maintain active fleets. Passage is expensive. Contracts are binding. Accidents are catastrophic.

**What This Means:**

The existence of these vessels demonstrates that the \u00e6ther can be **resisted, but not tamed**. All known methods rely on **containment, not control**.

---

## THE CATASTROPHE

### IV. The Mining Operation

At some point in the past, a dwarven civilization uncovered and mined a rare crystalline formation later termed **tuning crystals**.

#### What Happened

**Initial State:**
- At the time, the purpose of these crystals was unknown
- The mining operation was successful
- The dwarves extracted the crystals and transported them elsewhere
- The immediate consequences were subtle

**What Did NOT Happen:**
- Waygates continued to function
- No mass extinctions occurred
- No worlds vanished
- No cataclysmic explosion or dimensional collapse

#### The Gradual Unraveling

Instead, gradual anomalies emerged across multiple connected worlds.

**Observable Effects:**
- Landscapes shifted without geological cause
- Ruins appeared where none had stood
- Familiar locations subtly failed to align with memory or record
- Atmospheric and ecological irregularities became increasingly common
- The stars no longer aligned with recorded cycles

**The Pattern:**

At first, these events seemed unrelated\u2014local disturbances, isolated incidents, natural variation. But as reports accumulated across worlds, scholars began to recognize a pattern.

Something systemic was failing.

#### What the Crystals Were

Later scholarship concluded that the tuning crystals were not power sources, but **calibration structures**\u2014components that maintained alignment and synchronization between worlds already linked by the waygate network.

Their removal did not destroy the system.

It degraded it.

#### The True Nature of the Catastrophe

The catastrophe is best understood not as a single event, but as the beginning of an **ongoing condition: desynchronization**.

> Worlds did not break. They drifted.

The effects persist to this day.

---

### V. The Pilots

#### When They Appeared

Pilots began appearing only after the catastrophe.

No known world claims them as native. No historical records describe their existence prior to the event.

#### What Makes Them Different

**\u00c6ther Immunity:**

Pilots can traverse the \u00e6ther without:
- Shielding
- Reactors
- Sustaining rituals

They simply walk through it.

This ability is **unique and unexplained**.

No other known creature, race, or construct possesses this trait.

#### How They Are Perceived

Pilots are regarded everywhere as interlopers\u2014present, functional, but never fully belonging.

**Common Assumptions:**
- They are remnants of the catastrophe itself
- They are constructs or echoes rather than true living beings
- They are somehow connected to the desynchronization

**Unverified Theories:**
- Some believe pilots are survivors of a lost world
- Others claim they are walking fractures in reality
- A few suggest they were intentionally created as a response to the catastrophe

No theory has been proven.

#### What They Can Do

Pilots possess the unique ability to interface with **mechs**\u2014powerful armored constructs that amplify their already unusual capabilities.

This bond between pilot and mech is not fully understood, but it is observed to be:
- Instantaneous
- Intuitive
- Highly effective in combat

Pilots are sought after by factions across the worlds for this reason alone.

#### Why They Matter

In a fractured multiverse where travel is dangerous and resources are contested, pilots represent a strategic advantage.

They are:
- Immune to \u00e6theric exposure
- Capable of operating complex war machines
- Able to navigate between worlds without traditional infrastructure

This makes them valuable. And dangerous.

---

## THE CURRENT STATE OF THE WORLDS

### VI. The Fragmented Present

The catastrophe did not end the worlds. It scattered them.

#### What Changed

**Before:**
- Worlds existed in stable, predictable alignment
- Travel between them was routine
- Trade, diplomacy, and cultural exchange flourished

**After:**
- Alignment became unstable
- Distances between worlds fluctuate
- Some worlds drift closer; others recede into inaccessibility
- Entire civilizations have been isolated for generations

**The Result:**

The network of connected worlds has fractured into isolated clusters. Some maintain contact through waygates. Others rely on rare and expensive interworld vessels. Many have been cut off entirely.

#### Who Survived

Not all civilizations adapted equally.

**The Dominant Powers:**
- Advanced technological societies with access to interworld vessels
- Magic-rich cultures capable of sustaining protective fields
- Militarized factions that seized control of waygate access

**The Struggling:**
- Worlds without waygate access
- Civilizations dependent on trade routes that no longer function
- Populations stranded on drifting worlds

**The Lost:**
- Entire worlds whose waygates have ceased responding
- Civilizations that vanished during the early chaos
- Cultures erased by ecological collapse or factional war

#### The New Order

In the absence of stable connection, power consolidates around those who control:
- Waygate access
- Interworld vessels
- Strategic resources
- Pilot recruitment

Factions rise and fall. Alliances shift. War is constant.

---

### VII. Camelot: A World in Fracture

One of the most studied post-catastrophe worlds is **Camelot**.

#### What It Was

Before the catastrophe, Camelot was a thriving center of magic and governance. It hosted one of the largest and most stable waygates in the network, serving as a nexus for interworld diplomacy and trade.

#### What It Became

Following the catastrophe, Camelot experienced severe desynchronization.

**Observable Effects:**
- Entire regions phased in and out of alignment with the rest of the world
- Cities flickered between states of ruin and restoration
- The ruling authority collapsed as communication between territories became impossible
- Factional warfare erupted over control of the waygate

**Current State:**

Camelot is now a fractured battlefield. Multiple factions claim authority. The waygate remains functional, but access is contested. Pilots are recruited aggressively by all sides.

Scholars study Camelot as a microcosm of the larger multiverse: a world caught between what it was and what it might become.

---

# PART II: GAME SYSTEMS

## COMBAT ROLES & TRAIT LINES

### Core Design Philosophy

**Project Orion** employs a role-based combat system where each pilot specializes in a **Trait Line** that defines their battlefield identity. Unlike traditional class systems, trait lines are flexible frameworks that shape playstyle through resource prioritization and feat selection.

**Core Principles:**
- **Role Identity** \u2014 Each trait line has a clear battlefield purpose
- **Resource Dynamics** \u2014 Roles interpret Heat, Energy, and Threat differently
- **Feat Progression** \u2014 Five tiers of feats unlock specialized capabilities
- **Build Flexibility** \u2014 Multiple viable builds within each trait line

---

### Available Trait Lines
#### Warrior \u2014 Frontline Striker

**Identity:** Aggressive frontline damage dealer  
**Playstyle:** High damage output through weapon mastery and aggressive positioning

**Core Strengths:**
- Superior weapon damage scaling
- Heat management for sustained DPS
- Mobility for aggressive engagement

**Core Weaknesses:**
- Lower defensive stats
- Requires precise positioning
- Vulnerable when heat-capped

**Starting Loadout:**
- **Frame:** PNSY W416 "Warrior" Fighter Frame
- **Primary Weapon:** PNSY M-300 Hasta (Medium Lance)
- **Generator:** Basic combat reactor
- **Systems:** Offensive-focused subsystems

**Feat Categories:**
- **Weapon Mastery** \u2014 Enhanced damage, accuracy, critical hits
- **Heat Cycling** \u2014 Heat management and overdrive capabilities
- **Mobility** \u2014 Dash enhancements and positioning tools
- **Execution** \u2014 Finishing moves and low-health damage spikes

---

#### Guardian \u2014 Defensive Anchor (Paladin)

**Identity:** Protective tank with ally support capabilities  
**Playstyle:** Frontline defender who draws aggro and shields allies

**Core Strengths:**
- High durability and threat generation
- Energy-based defensive abilities
- Ally protection and healing

**Core Weaknesses:**
- Lower damage output
- Energy-dependent sustainability
- Vulnerable to energy disruption

**Starting Loadout:**
- **Frame:** Dawnforge Guardian Coreplate
- **Primary Weapon:** Defensive armament
- **Generator:** High-capacity energy reactor
- **Systems:** Shield generators and threat amplifiers

**Feat Categories:**
- **Aegis Protocols** \u2014 Shield strength and coverage
- **Radiant Recovery** \u2014 Healing and regeneration
- **Threat Command** \u2014 Aggro manipulation
- **Righteous Fury** \u2014 Damage scaling from defensive stats

---

#### Marauder \u2014 Aggressive Bruiser

**Identity:** High-durability brawler with burst damage  
**Playstyle:** Sustained combat through armor and aggressive trading

**Core Strengths:**
- High armor and health pool
- Heat-fueled damage spikes
- Natural threat generation through aggression

**Core Weaknesses:**
- Lower mobility
- Heat-dependent damage
- Vulnerable to kiting

**Starting Loadout:**
- **Frame:** Fire & Ice Fortress Coreplate
- **Primary Weapon:** Heavy melee or close-range armament
- **Generator:** High-heat tolerance reactor
- **Systems:** Armor plating and heat sinks

**Feat Categories:**
- **Fortified Assault** \u2014 Armor scaling and durability
- **Thermal Overdrive** \u2014 Heat-based damage amplification
- **Relentless Advance** \u2014 Gap closers and movement
- **Brutal Momentum** \u2014 Damage scaling from consecutive hits

---

### Feat Progression System

Feats are unlocked across **five tiers** as pilots gain experience and master their trait line.

**Tier I \u2014 Foundation** (Early Game)
- Basic role identity
- Core resource interactions
- Fundamental combat enhancements

**Tier II \u2014 Specialization** (Mid Game)
- Role-defining capabilities
- Secondary resource synergies
- Build divergence begins

**Tier III \u2014 Mastery** (Mid-Late Game)
- Advanced techniques
- Cross-resource interactions
- Signature abilities

**Tier IV \u2014 Dominance** (Late Game)
- High-impact capabilities
- Multi-resource manipulation
- Build-defining powers

**Tier V \u2014 Transcendence** (End Game)
- Ultimate abilities
- Role pinnacle expression
- Game-changing effects

---

## RESOURCE SYSTEM

Resources in **Project Orion** define the mech's behavioral identity. While **structural stats** set physical limits, resources determine how builds *feel* in combat.

### Core Resources

#### \ud83d\udd25 Heat

Heat governs cadence, reactor strain, and overdrive potential.

**Mechanics:**
- Builds with weapon use and reactor strain
- Dissipates gradually when not actively generating
- Reaching max heat causes **reactor overload** (forced cooldown)

**Playstyle Impact:**
- **High Heat Tolerance** \u2014 Burst damage specialists, risk-reward gameplay
- **Low Heat Management** \u2014 Sustained DPS, safe operation
- **Heat Manipulation** \u2014 Builds that weaponize heat levels

**Role Interpretations:**
- **Warrior:** Resource to spend for damage
- **Guardian:** Risk to manage while maintaining threat
- **Marauder:** Fuel for offensive power spikes

---

#### \ud83d\udd0b Energy

Energy governs reactor pool, regeneration, and subsystem uptime.

**Mechanics:**
- Passive regeneration over time
- Consumed by active abilities and sustained systems
- Running out causes **energy starvation** (reduced capabilities)

**Playstyle Impact:**
- **High Energy Pool** \u2014 Sustained ability usage, always active
- **Low Energy Economy** \u2014 Careful resource management, burst windows
- **Energy Regen Focus** \u2014 Near-infinite uptime on key systems

**Role Interpretations:**
- **Warrior:** Secondary sustain for mobility and burst
- **Guardian:** Primary resource for shields and healing
- **Marauder:** Tertiary resource, low priority

---

#### \ud83c\udfaf Threat

Threat governs enemy awareness, aggro generation, and battlefield presence.

**Mechanics:**
- Increases with damage dealt and defensive actions
- Decreases gradually when not engaging
- High threat draws enemy focus

**Playstyle Impact:**
- **High Threat** \u2014 Tank role, enemy magnet
- **Low Threat** \u2014 Stealth striker, avoids focus
- **Threat Manipulation** \u2014 Tactical control over enemy targeting

**Role Interpretations:**
- **Warrior:** Byproduct of damage, managed to avoid focus
- **Guardian:** Primary tool for protecting allies
- **Marauder:** Natural consequence of aggressive playstyle

---

### Resource Priority Chains

Each role prioritizes resources differently, creating distinct playstyle identities.

**Warrior \u2014 Heat > Energy > Threat**
- Heat fuels damage output
- Energy sustains mobility and burst windows
- Threat emerges as consequence, must be managed

**Guardian \u2014 Threat > Energy > Heat**
- Threat is primary tool for protecting allies
- Energy sustains defensive abilities
- Heat is managed to avoid overload

**Marauder \u2014 Heat = Threat > Energy**
- Heat and Threat both fuel offensive pressure
- Natural synergy between damage and aggro
- Energy is minimal concern

---

## STRUCTURAL STATS

Structural stats define the physical limits and capabilities of the mech chassis.

### Primary Stats

#### Armor
**Function:** Damage reduction and durability  
**Impact:** Determines how much punishment the mech can absorb  
**Scaling:** Increases with chassis tier and armor components

#### Hull Points (HP)
**Function:** Total health pool  
**Impact:** Determines survival threshold  
**Scaling:** Base value from chassis, bonuses from components

#### Mobility
**Function:** Movement speed and dash capability  
**Impact:** Positioning and kiting ability  
**Scaling:** Influenced by leg components and weight distribution

#### Load Capacity
**Function:** Maximum equipment weight  
**Impact:** Limits what can be equipped simultaneously  
**Scaling:** Set by chassis, modified by frame components

---

### Derived Stats

#### Stability
**Function:** Resistance to knockback and stagger  
**Impact:** Determines ability to maintain position under fire  
**Derived From:** Armor + Weight

#### Sensor Range
**Function:** Detection radius for enemies and objectives  
**Impact:** Awareness and tactical information  
**Derived From:** Sensor components and chassis type

#### Heat Capacity
**Function:** Maximum heat before overload  
**Impact:** Determines burst potential vs sustained output  
**Derived From:** Reactor + Cooling Systems

#### Energy Pool
**Function:** Maximum stored energy  
**Impact:** Ability uptime and sustained performance  
**Derived From:** Generator + Capacitors

---

## ITEMIZATION & EQUIPMENT

### Acquisition Methods

**Blueprints & Schematics**
- Found in dungeons and combat zones
- Unlock crafting for new gear types
- Rare blueprints enable unique builds

**Material Scavenging**
- Collect ores, alloys, and magitech components
- Used for crafting and upgrading
- Different regions yield different materials

**Faction Rewards**
- Completing missions grants faction-specific items
- Alignment choices unlock unique equipment sets
- Reputation gating for advanced gear

**World Exploration**
- Hidden caches contain rare items
- Environmental puzzles reward discovery
- Encourages replayability and thorough exploration

---

### Equipment Categories

#### Armor Components
External plating and mounts defining durability and appearance.

**Slots:**
- Head Optics
- Torso Plating
- Arm Stabilizers
- Leg Platforms

**Properties:**
- Armor value
- Load capacity modification
- Sensor integration
- Aesthetic customization

---

#### Frame Components
Internal systems that define mech identity and capability.

**Core Systems:**
- **Generator** \u2014 Energy pool and regeneration
- **Reactor** \u2014 Heat capacity and power output
- **Cooling System** \u2014 Heat dissipation rate
- **Sensor Suite** \u2014 Detection and targeting

**Advanced Systems:**
- **Propulsion Unit** \u2014 Mobility enhancement
- **Targeting Computer** \u2014 Accuracy bonuses
- **Threat Amplifier** \u2014 Aggro modification
- **Recovery System** \u2014 HP regeneration

---

#### Weapons
Offensive armaments defining combat approach.

**Weapon Classes:**
- **Main Weapons** \u2014 Primary damage source
  - Heavy Lance
  - Medium Lance
  - Light Sidearm
  - Heavy Gun
  - Launcher
  - Special Weapon

**Weapon Properties:**
- Damage type (Physical, Energy, Hybrid)
- Heat generation per shot
- Energy consumption
- Threat generation
- Range and accuracy

---

#### Auxiliaries
Tactical subsystems expanding mech capabilities.

**Types:**
- Shield Emitters
- Cloaking Devices
- Drones
- Deployable Turrets
- Utility Systems

**Characteristics:**
- Active or passive operation
- Energy consumption patterns
- Cooldown mechanics
- Synergy with trait lines

---

#### Utilities
Consumables and deployables for situational advantage.

**Categories:**
- Coolant Packs (emergency heat dump)
- Grenades (area denial, damage, utility)
- Mines (defensive positioning)
- Ammo Reloads (extended combat)
- Repair Kits (emergency HP recovery)

---

### Crafting & Upgrading

**Crafting System:**
- Requires blueprint + materials
- Success rate influenced by pilot level
- Can produce basic to advanced gear

**Upgrading System:**
- Improve existing equipment stats
- Requires rare materials
- Unlocks additional mod slots

**Modification System:**
- Install mods into equipment slots
- Mods provide specialized bonuses
- Can be swapped to adapt builds

---

## FEAT SYSTEM DEEP DIVE

Feats are permanent unlocks that define and specialize a pilot's capabilities within their trait line.

### Feat Structure

**Universal Properties:**
- Unlocked through experience and progression
- Cannot be unlearned (permanent choices)
- Limited feat points encourage specialization
- Synergies reward coherent build strategies

---

### Warrior Feat Lines

#### Tier I \u2014 Foundation Feats

**Weapon Focus**
- +10% damage with equipped weapon type
- Reduces heat generation by 5%

**Combat Momentum**
- Movement speed increases by 15% for 3 seconds after dealing damage

**Precise Strikes**
- +8% critical hit chance
- Critical hits reduce weapon cooldown by 0.2 seconds

**Heat Discipline**
- +15% heat capacity
- Heat dissipation starts 1 second earlier

---

#### Tier II \u2014 Specialization Feats

**Blade Dancer** (Melee Focus)
- Melee weapons gain +20% attack speed
- Consecutive melee hits increase damage by 5% (stacks 3x)

**Sharpshooter** (Ranged Focus)
- Ranged weapons gain +25% accuracy at long range
- Standing still for 2 seconds grants +15% damage

**Thermal Surge**
- When above 75% heat, gain +20% damage
- Taking damage at high heat triggers 3-second damage buff

**Executioner's Edge**
- Deal +30% damage to enemies below 25% HP
- Killing blows restore 10% heat capacity

---

#### Tier III \u2014 Mastery Feats

**Overdrive Protocol**
- Activate to gain +40% damage for 8 seconds
- Generates maximum heat
- 60-second cooldown

**Relentless Assault**
- Every 4th hit against the same target deals double damage
- Counter resets if target changes

**Phase Strike**
- Dash attacks deal +50% damage and ignore 30% armor
- Costs 25% energy

**Critical Mastery**
- Critical hits deal +50% damage (up from base +25%)
- Critical hits restore 5% energy

---

#### Tier IV \u2014 Dominance Feats

**Apex Predator**
- +15% damage for each enemy within 15 meters (max 45%)
- Kills extend all active buffs by 2 seconds

**Thermal Cascade**
- Heat generation increases damage by 1% per 2% current heat
- At maximum heat, damage increased by 50%

**Warrior's Fury**
- When below 30% HP, gain +35% damage and +25% attack speed
- Heat generation reduced by 50% while active

**Death from Above**
- Aerial attacks deal +100% damage
- Landing near enemies stuns them for 1 second

---

#### Tier V \u2014 Transcendence Feats

**Ultimate: Blade Storm**
- Unleash a devastating 5-second attack sequence
- Attack speed increased by 200%
- Heat generation suppressed
- 120-second cooldown

**Ultimate: Perfect Strike**
- Next attack deals 500% damage and cannot miss
- Ignores all armor and shields
- 90-second cooldown

# MECHANICS ÔÇö V1
### Project Orion | Combat Systems Reference

---

## TABLE OF CONTENTS

1. [Core Concepts](#1-core-concepts)
2. [Action System](#2-action-system)
3. [Skill System](#3-skill-system)
4. [Reload System](#4-reload-system)
5. [Weapon Swap](#5-weapon-swap)
6. [Cooldown System](#6-cooldown-system)
7. [Weapon Definition Schema](#7-weapon-definition-schema)
8. [Reference Example ÔÇö Gladius (Rifle)](#8-reference-example--gladius-rifle)

---

## 1. CORE CONCEPTS

### Action
The atomic unit of a moveset. An action has a base duration and a typed payload (hit, burst, effect, etc.). Actions are not modified at the definition level ÔÇö modifications are applied at the skill slot reference level, leaving the source action unchanged.

### Action Modifier
Applied to a skill slot's action reference, not the action definition itself. Controls duration override, repeat count, and timing split. The source action is always preserved.

### Library
An optional pool of swappable action variants scoped to a weapon. Used when a skill needs dynamic or replaceable actions (e.g. burst patterns that change with mods). If no library is referenced, actions in the skill sequence are inline and fixed.

### Skill
One of five slots per weapon, indexed `[0..4]`.
- **Skill 0** ÔÇö Auto-attack. Single or multi-action chain. Repeatable.
- **Skills 1ÔÇô4** ÔÇö Unique, weapon-specific. Variable type and behavior.

### Moveset
The complete set of five skills for a weapon. A full moveset defines the weapon's combat identity. Skills can be altered by weapon modifications.

### Cooldown
A timed lockout on a specific slot, state, or system. Governed by a strict isolation rule ÔÇö see [Section 6](#6-cooldown-system).

---

## 2. ACTION SYSTEM

### Action Definition

```
action {
  id:             string
  type:           enum [strike, burst, beam, special]
  base_duration:  float (sec)
  payload:        type-specific (see below)
}
```

### Payload Types

```
// Strike ÔÇö melee
strike_payload {
  anim_tag:     string     // animation identifier e.g. "swing_1"
  hit_count:    int        // hits per execution (default: 1)
  damage_mult:  float
}

// Burst ÔÇö ranged
burst_payload {
  shot_count:   int
  damage_mult:  float
}
```

### Action Slot Reference
Actions are referenced inside skill sequences via an `action_ref`. This is where per-slot modifications are applied.

```
action_ref {
  action_id:          string
  repeat:             int     // default: 1
  duration_override:  float | null
    // null + repeat > 1: auto = base_duration / repeat
    // explicit value: overrides base for this execution only
}
```

### Double Strike Pattern
When a modifier makes an action a double strike, the action is referenced twice in the same slot at half duration each. This preserves total slot time and creates two independent interrupt windows instead of one longer uninterruptable animation.

```
// Base ÔÇö no modifier
{ action_id: "swing_1", repeat: 1 }
// Ôćĺ 1 hit at 0.5 sec | 1 interrupt window

// With double-strike modifier
{ action_id: "swing_1", repeat: 2, duration_override: null }
// Ôćĺ 2 hits at 0.25 sec each | 2 interrupt windows
// Ôćĺ total time unchanged: 0.5 sec
// Ôćĺ same animation at 2├Ś speed ÔÇö no new asset required
// Ôćĺ no hyper armor or i-frames unless explicitly defined
```

**Rule:** `duration_override: null` with `repeat > 1` always auto-divides base duration equally across repetitions, preserving total slot time. If a modifier is intended to add a hit *and* extend total time, an explicit `duration_override` must be set.

---

## 3. SKILL SYSTEM

### Skill Definition

```
skill {
  index:     int [0..4]
  type:      enum [chain, single, held, cooldown]
  sequence:  action_ref[]       // ordered execution list
  cooldown:  float | null       // null for skill_0 (auto-attack)
  library:   library_id | null  // null = all actions are inline
}
```

### Library Definition

```
actions_library {
  id:       string
  actions:  action[]
}
```

Libraries are scoped to a weapon. A skill references a library only when its actions need to be dynamic or swappable via modifications. Most skills use inline fixed actions and do not require a library.

---

## 4. RELOAD SYSTEM

Reload is an automated cooldown state. It is **not** a skill slot and does not consume any of the five moveset slots.

### Trigger
- **Auto** ÔÇö fires when ammo reaches zero
- **Manual** ÔÇö player-activated (default keybind: `R`)
- **Both** ÔÇö default behavior

### Duration Calculation

**Mode: `per_shot` (default)**
```
reload_duration = shots_fired_since_last_reload ├Ś scalar
```
Partial chains cost partial reload. Only actual shots fired are counted.

**Mode: `forced_full` (balance flag)**
```
reload_duration = max_shots ├Ś scalar
```
Always costs the full magazine reload regardless of shots fired. Applied to specific weapons as a balance decision. Punishes partial chain use and rewards committing to a full sequence before reloading or swapping.

### Reload Cooldown Definition

```
reload_cooldown {
  id:            "reload_{weapon_id}"
  type:          cooldown
  mode:          enum [per_shot, forced_full]
  scalar:        float              // sec per shot
  max_shots:     int                // required for forced_full mode
  trigger:       enum [auto, manual, both]
  keybind:       string             // default "R"
}
```

---

## 5. WEAPON SWAP

Weapon swap is a global player action that switches between equipped weapon sets.

```
weapon_swap_cooldown {
  id:             "weapon_swap"
  type:           cooldown
  base_duration:  5.0 sec
  scope:          global
    // one shared timer ÔÇö not per-weapon
    // modifiable by cooldown effects (see Section 6)
}
```

### Persistence Rule
Cooldowns are bound to the **weapon**, not the active equipment slot. When a weapon is swapped out:
- All cooldowns on that weapon continue decrementing
- Cooldowns do not reset
- Cooldowns do not pause

When the weapon is re-equipped, its cooldowns reflect actual elapsed time. Weapon swap cannot be used to circumvent or reset reload cooldowns.

---

## 6. COOLDOWN SYSTEM

### Isolation Rule
Cooldowns are independent of all other game systems. They cannot be paused, interrupted, reset, or altered by any effect except those explicitly typed in the **modifier whitelist** below.

The following effect categories have **no interaction** with cooldowns:
- Crowd control (stun, stagger, freeze, silence, root, etc.)
- Damage effects
- Status effects
- Skill effects (unless explicitly cooldown-typed)

### Modifier Whitelist

Only two effect types may modify a cooldown:

```
cooldown_modifier {
  type:     enum [reduction, increase]
    // 'reset' does not exist as an effect type

  value:    float (0.0 ÔÇô 1.0)
    // 0.50 = 50% reduction or increase
    // 1.00 = 100% (rare ÔÇö see note below)
    // values > 1.0 are illegal

  window: {
    duration:  float (sec)    // how long this modifier is active
    trigger:   string         // activation condition
  }

  target:   string            // specific cooldown_id, or "all" (rare)
  stacking: multiplicative    // always ÔÇö no exceptions
}
```

### Stacking Formula
All cooldown modifiers stack **multiplicatively**. Each reduction applies to the remaining value after prior reductions, not to the base. This enforces diminishing returns by construction ÔÇö no special cap logic required.

```
effective_cooldown = base ├Ś (1 - r1) ├Ś (1 - r2) ├Ś (1 - r3) ...
```

### Stacking Reference Table

| Reductions Active | Value Each | Result on 3.0 sec base | Absolute Gain |
|---|---|---|---|
| 1├Ś 50% | 0.50 | 1.500 sec | Ôłĺ1.500 sec |
| 2├Ś 50% | 0.50 | 0.750 sec | Ôłĺ0.750 sec |
| 3├Ś 50% | 0.50 | 0.375 sec | Ôłĺ0.375 sec |
| 4├Ś 50% | 0.50 | 0.188 sec | Ôłĺ0.188 sec |
| 1├Ś 100% | 1.00 | 0.000 sec | Ôłĺ3.000 sec |
| 50% + 100% | ÔÇö | 0.000 sec | 100% dominates |

Each additional reduction of the same value yields less absolute benefit than the last. Stacking never reaches zero unless an explicit `value: 1.0` effect is applied.

### Implementation Note
Additive stacking (combining percentages before applying) is explicitly **not supported**. Two 50% reductions must be applied sequentially ÔÇö `base ├Ś 0.5 ├Ś 0.5` ÔÇö never combined as `base ├Ś (1 - 1.0)`. This must be enforced at the system level, not assumed from design intent alone.

### Design Notes
- **100% reduction** effects exist but are rare, niche, and situationally specific. The exploit vector is `window.duration`, not `value` ÔÇö a 100% reduction for 10 seconds on a short cooldown is significantly stronger than the same value for 0.5 seconds.
- **`target: "all"`** modifier scope is substantially stronger than targeted reduction and should be restricted to high-tier feats or items (Tier IV minimum recommended).
- `window.duration` is the primary balance lever for cooldown reduction effects. It is distinct from `value` and should be tuned independently.

---

## 7. WEAPON DEFINITION SCHEMA

Full schema combining all systems above.

```
weapon {
  name:             string
  class:            string         // Rifle, Melee, Launcher, etc.

  library:          actions_library | null

  reload_cooldown: {
    id:             "reload_{weapon_id}"
    type:           cooldown
    mode:           enum [per_shot, forced_full]
    scalar:         float
    max_shots:      int | null     // required if mode: forced_full
    trigger:        enum [auto, manual, both]
    keybind:        string
  }

  moveset: {
    skill_0:  skill    // auto-attack chain
    skill_1:  skill
    skill_2:  skill
    skill_3:  skill
    skill_4:  skill
  }
}
```

---

## 8. REFERENCE EXAMPLE ÔÇö GLADIUS (RIFLE)

```
weapon {
  name:   "Gladius"
  class:  Rifle

  library: {
    id: "gladius_burst_lib"
    actions: [
      { id: "burst_1", type: burst, base_duration: 0.5, payload: { shot_count: 3 } },
      { id: "burst_2", type: burst, base_duration: 0.5, payload: { shot_count: 2 } },
      { id: "burst_3", type: burst, base_duration: 0.5, payload: { shot_count: 4 } },
    ]
  }

  reload_cooldown: {
    id:        "reload_gladius"
    type:      cooldown
    mode:      per_shot
    scalar:    0.35           // sec per shot fired
    trigger:   both
    keybind:   "R"
    // forced_full: false
  }

  moveset: {

    skill_0: {
      type:     chain
      library:  "gladius_burst_lib"
      sequence: [
        { action_id: "burst_1" },    // 0.5 sec | 3 shots
        { action_id: "burst_1" },    // 0.5 sec | 3 shots
        { action_id: "burst_1" },    // 0.5 sec | 3 shots
      ]
      cooldown: null
      // full chain: 1.5 sec | 9 shots
      // reload (full chain): 9 ├Ś 0.35 = 3.15 sec
      // reload (1 burst only): 3 ├Ś 0.35 = 1.05 sec
      // reload continues on Gladius if weapon is swapped mid-cooldown
    }

    skill_1: UNDEFINED
    skill_2: UNDEFINED
    skill_3: UNDEFINED
    skill_4: UNDEFINED
  }
}
```

---

## VERIFICATION STATUS

**TIER 1 (Documented in orion_story_v1.txt):**
- Border town location: between orc camp and interior Camelot
- Bedivere's corpse findable en route
- Boss encounters: Percival, Tristan, Bors
- Large explorable area + massive deep dungeon
- No safezone designation
- NPC hostility mechanic: "grail sickness"
- Dynamic invasion system: orc raiding parties

**TIER 2 (Inferred from loredoc.md - Camelot section):**
- Post-catastrophe state: desynchronized regions
- Visual flickering between ruin/restoration states
- Collapsed central authority
- Factional warfare context
- Waygate control as political objective

## BORDER TOWN EXPANSION

### ENVIRONMENTAL STRUCTURE

**Settlement Layout:**

**Outer Perimeter** (Contested Zone)
- Collapsed stone walls, partially rebuilt with scrap
- Orc siege equipment abandoned mid-assault
- Burnt-out waystation buildings
- Player spawn point if arriving from M00-THE-BOG

**Market District** (Central Hub)
- Half-functioning marketplace
- NPC merchant zones (hostile/neutral state fluctuates)
- Visible desynchronization effects: buildings phase between intact/ruined states
- Container caches: weapon parts, consumables, blueprints

**Barracks Quarter** (Combat Zone)
- Former knight garrison, now factional holdout
- Percival/Tristan/Bors patrol routes originate here
- Heavy enemy density
- High-tier loot in armory containers

**Cathedral District** (Atmospheric/Lore Zone)
- Grail iconography, corrupted religious imagery
- Grail sickness visual cues: NPCs with glowing eyes, erratic behavior
- Lore documents explaining catastrophe impact on Camelot

**Dungeon Entrance** (Gateway to Deep Dungeon)
- Guarded by elite enemies OR locked behind quest requirement
- Visual: descending stone shaft with aetheric energy leaking upward

---

### HOSTILE NPC BEHAVIOR SYSTEM

**Grail Sickness Mechanic:**

**State 1: Neutral (25% baseline)**
- NPC will trade, provide dialogue
- Grail sickness symptoms visible but controlled

**State 2: Agitated (50% probability)**
- NPC dialogue becomes hostile
- Will attack if player loiters too long (15-second timer)
- Drops standard loot

**State 3: Feral (25% probability)**
- Immediate aggro on sight
- Enhanced stats (+25% damage, +50% movement speed)
- Drops grail-corrupted crafting materials

**Environmental Trigger:**
- Orc raid invasion forces ALL NPCs into Feral state for duration
- Creates layered threat: player vs orcs vs corrupted NPCs

---

### BOSS ENCOUNTER DESIGN

**Percival, Tristan, Bors** (3 Mini-Bosses, Can Fight Individually or Together)

**Percival** - Grail Knight (Heavy Tank)
- **Resource Priority:** Threat > Energy > Heat
- **Behavior:** Guardian-archetype, protects Tristan/Bors if fought together
- **Mechanics:**
  - Shield wall stance: reduces damage, reflects projectiles
  - Grail Regeneration: passive HP regen when below 50%
  - Righteous Charge: gap-closer with knockback
- **Loot:** Guardian Frame Blueprint + "Grail Fragment" (quest item)

**Tristan** - Corrupted Ranger (DPS/Ranged)
- **Resource Priority:** Energy > Heat > Threat
- **Behavior:** Kiting, maintains distance, punishes melee rushdown
- **Mechanics:**
  - Longbow Volley: high-damage ranged attack pattern
  - Smoke Retreat: teleports to edge of arena when cornered
  - Grail Sight: reveals player position through walls
- **Loot:** Advanced Sensor Suite + "Corrupted Shard" (crafting material)

**Bors** - Berserk Striker (High-Risk Aggro)
- **Resource Priority:** Heat > Threat > Energy
- **Behavior:** Marauder-archetype, relentless aggression
- **Mechanics:**
  - Fury Stacks: gains +10% damage per hit landed (max 10 stacks)
  - Grail Overload: at 50% HP, enters overdrive (immune to heat penalties)
  - Execution Lunge: one-shot ability if player below 20% HP
- **Loot:** Heavy Lance "Camlann's Ruin" + Armor Plating Blueprint

**Combined Fight Bonuses:**
- Fighting all 3 simultaneously grants "Knight's Oath" feat (+10% damage vs Camelot enemies)
- Unique dialogue sequence reveals lore about grail corruption

---

### ORC RAIDING PARTY SYSTEM

**Dynamic Invasion Trigger:**
- 15% chance every 5 minutes of exploration
- Announced by war horn sound + red visual pulse
- Blocks zone exit until cleared OR player escapes to dungeon entrance

**Invasion Composition:**
- 8-12 orc grunts (basic melee)
- 2-4 orc rangers (ranged harassment)
- 1 orc chieftain (mini-boss, drops map fragments)

**Tactical Layer:**
- Orcs prioritize attacking NPCs first
- Player can exploit chaos: loot NPC corpses, scavenge while enemies distracted
- Successfully defending town (killing all orcs before NPCs die) grants reputation bonus with surviving NPCs Ôćĺ temporary safezone effect

---

### DUNGEON ENTRANCE DESIGN

**Visual Presentation:**
- Massive stone staircase descending into darkness
- Aetheric mist rising from below (similar to M00-THE-BOG aesthetic)
- Grail symbols carved into walls, glowing faintly

**Access Requirements (Pick One Design):**

**Option A: Combat Gate**
- Must defeat Percival, Tristan, AND Bors to unlock
- Door opens after collecting all 3 "Grail Fragments"

**Option B: Exploration Gate**
- Must find 3 hidden switches scattered throughout border town
- Rewards thorough exploration, avoids forced combat

**Option C: Reputation Gate**
- Must achieve neutral standing with town NPCs (survive multiple orc raids without looting NPC corpses)
- Ethical constraint, aligns with narrative themes

---

### LOOT & PROGRESSION HOOKS

**Border Town Unique Items:**

**Blueprints:**
- "Camelot Knight Frame" (Guardian-focused chassis)
- "Grail-Touched Plating" (armor with HP regen passive)
- "Orc Breaker Lance" (high knockback, anti-infantry)

**Consumables:**
- Grail Water (corrupted healing item: restores 50% HP but generates heat)
- Orc War Paint (temporary +15% damage vs humanoid enemies)

**Quest Items:**
- Bedivere's Signet Ring (found on corpse, required for dungeon subplot)
- Map Fragment 2/3 (completes map from M01-ORC-ENCAMPMENT)

---

### ATMOSPHERIC TOUCHPOINTS

**Desynchronization Visual Effects:**
- Buildings flicker between states every 10-15 seconds
- NPCs occasionally phase through walls (visual only, doesn't affect gameplay)
- Time-of-day cycles rapidly (day/night shifts within minutes)

**Audio Design:**
- Distant screams (grail sickness victims)
- Orc war drums (foreshadows invasion)
- Cathedral bells ringing arrhythmically (desynchronization motif)

**Environmental Storytelling:**
- Corpses in knight armor scattered throughout
- Orc graffiti over Camelot heraldry
- Burnt grail tapestries
- Overturned market stalls with rotting goods

---

## INTEGRATION WITH EXISTING SYSTEMS

- Map fragments merge: orc camp map + border town map = complete regional map
- Reveals waygate location in Camelot interior (next zone)

**Connection to Deep Dungeon:**
- Dungeon serves as skill check before waygate access
- Contains lore documents explaining tuning crystal catastrophe
- Final boss drops "Camelot Waygate Key"
